 The campaigning in the northeastern state of Mizoram came to an end on Monday
 28 november ko hone vaale matdaan main visthapit bru votaron kaa mudda rajya ke sarkaar gathan main ahm bhoomika nibhaa saktaa he
 The Election Commission has set up polling booths in Kanhamun village on mizoram-tripura border for the last 21 years for Bru tribal voters in refugee camps in Tripura
 jabaki isse pehle bru sharnaarthi camp se hi postal bailat ke jariye apane matadhikaar kaa prayog karte the
 Why Principal Secretary Home and Chief Electoral Officer? Actually, in the wake of Mizoram Assembly elections, former Chief Electoral Officer (CEO) SB Shashank had allowed voters of the Bru community registered in Tripura relief camps to exercise their vote from there
 jiske baad saamaajik or raajnneetik sanghathanon ne shashaank ke khilaaf pradarshan kiya tha
 The protest was so fierce that the Election Commission office was set ablaze by protesters
 isse rajdhani izol samet puure rajya main saamaanya janajivan ast-vyast ho gaya tha

 Earlier Mizoram Chief Home Secretary Lalununmawiya Chuango opposed the initiative of arranging voting for the Bru refugees of Mizoram in the refugee camps in Tripura
